<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сердечный.html>серде́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">serdéčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> heart</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cordial, heartfelt</li>
<li>cardiac</li>
<li>amorous</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> love</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердиться.html>серди́ться</a> (3387)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сердить.html>серди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">serdítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сердиться.html>серди́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">serdítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассердиться.html>рассерди́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be angry
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1960</b>,  Василий Семёнович Гроссман (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vasily_Grossman" class="extiw" title="w:Vasily Grossman">Vasily Semyonovich Grossman</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>Жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>судьба́</a></cite>, part 3, chapter 42 |  translated as Robert Chandler, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Life_and_Fate" class="extiw" title="w:Life and Fate">Life and Fate</a></cite>, New York Review of Books, 1985:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сердиться.html>серди́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> людми́лу никола́евну <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:равнодушие.html>равноду́шие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> че́хову, <a href = vnd.unilang:подозревать.html>подозрева́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́гих</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чеховский.html>че́ховских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассказ.html>расска́зов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ла</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vsju žiznʹ on <b>serdílsja</b> na Ljudmílu Nikolájevnu za ravnodúšije k Čéxovu, podozrevál, što mnógix čéxovskix rasskázov oná ne čitála.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He had always <b>resented</b> Lyudmila's indifference towards Chekhov; he suspected she hadn't even read most of his stories.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сердить.html>серди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">serdítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***сердце.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a> (327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сьрдьце</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sĭrdĭce</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sьrdьce</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱr̥d-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">heart</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">core</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sérdce</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>сердца́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>серде́ц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> heart
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a></b> — фибро́зно-мы́шечный <a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>о́рган</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:обеспечивающий.html>обеспе́чивающий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ток.html>ток</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кро́ви</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровеносный.html>кровено́сным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сосуд.html>сосу́дам</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Sérdce</b> — fibrózno-mýšečnyj órgan, obespéčivajuščij <a href = vnd.unilang:ток.html>tok</a> króvi po krovenósnym sosúdam.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The heart is a fibromuscular organ, which supplies blood flow through blood vessels.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>temper</li>
<li>anger</li>
<li>darling, love, sweetheart</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сереющий.html>сере́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">seréjuščij</span>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сержант.html>сержа́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">seržánt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сержант.html>сержа́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сержант.html>сержа́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сержант.html>сержа́нтов</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:серный.html>се́рный</a> (13773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́ра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">séra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:серный.html>се́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sérnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sulfur; sulfuric</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">серноки́слый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sernokíslyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***серп.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:серп.html>серп</a> (11541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sьrpъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sr̥p-</i>. Cognate with {{cog|ru|<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">срьпъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">srĭpŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sickle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">сърп</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sǎrp</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">srp</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">sierp</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">סערפּ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">serp</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; and with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">sirpis</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">ἅρπη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ἅrpi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sarpō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru">серп</strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">serp</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">серпа́</b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">серпы́</b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">серпо́в</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sickle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">се́рп и мо́лот</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sérp i mólot</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hammer and sickle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>crescent</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>серп</b>
</p><p>Существительное, неодушевлённое, мужской род, 2-е склонение (тип склонения 1b  по классификации А. А. Зализняка).
</p><p>Корень: <b>-серп-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение">Значение</span></h4>
<ol><li>сельскохозяйственное орудие для срезания растений, крепящийся на ручке дугообразный нож с острой зазубренной внутренней кромкой <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen">Американцы работают жатвенными машинами, которые они сами и выдумали; говорят, у них об <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">серпах</span> и косах уже забыли. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%AD%D0%BD%D0%B3%D0%B5%D0%BB%D1%8C%D0%B3%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B4%D1%82,_%D0%90%D0%BB%D0%B5%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4%D1%80_%D0%9D%D0%B8%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:Энгельгардт, Александр Николаевич">А. Н. Энгельгардт</a>, «Письма из деревни (1872–1887 гг.)»<span class="citation-source"> </span></i></span></span></span></li>
<li>геральдический символ в виде стилизованного изображения этого орудия <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen">Слева молот, справа <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">серп</span> — это наш советский герб. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><span class="citation-source"> </span></i></span></span></span></li>
<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="переносное значение">перен.</span> луна в первой четверти <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen">Лунный <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">серп</span> глядит в окно. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><span class="citation-source"> </span></i></span></span></span></li></ol>

<ol><li>—</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сертификат.html>сертифика́т</a> (14186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сертификат.html>сертифика́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sertifikát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сертификат.html>сертифика́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сертификат.html>сертифика́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сертификат.html>сертифика́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>certificate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сертификат.html>сертифика́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:качество.html>ка́чества</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sertifikát</b> káčestva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">certificate of quality</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сертификат.html>сертифика́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствие.html>соотве́тствия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sertifikát</b> sootvétstvija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">certification of conformity</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">депози́тный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сертификат.html>сертифика́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">depozítnyj <b>sertifikát</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">certificate of deposit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сертификат.html>сертифика́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:происхождение.html>происхожде́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sertifikát</b> o proisxoždénii továra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">certificate of origin</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
